posted:Posted May 25, 2024
msg:Wenzhou on a business trip, staying at Ruijin Hotel, you can see it from a distance in the car, the building is very luxurious, the driver also said that this is the best hotel in Yongjia, north of Oujiang River. As soon as I got off the car, there was a very handsome security uncle to help move the luggage. I was in a hurry and didn't have time to take pictures. The lobby is decorated very stylishly and tastefully, all made of marble. The handsome guy at the front desk always had a smile on his face, and took the initiative to help us send the luggage to the elevator.
Entering the room, there are very large glass windows, the lighting is particularly good, the curtains are smart, and they open automatically when entering. The room is equipped with Xiaodu, which can voice control the equipment in the room. There is also a table card for the use of the introduction at the head of the bed. The mattress and pillow are very comfortable. The two of us are together, and we sleep from ten o'clock to dawn, deep sleep, and get up at six in the morning to go to the gym on the sixth floor to exercise again.
Breakfast is on the top floor of the 23rd floor, a whole floor, with noodles, Yongjia special glutinous rice, noodles, wontons, hot dishes, cold dishes, seafood, adding up to dozens of choices, which is completely the level of luxury buffets in first-tier cities, and the taste is quite good. The breakfast room is all made of viewing glass all around, with a clear view. There is a mountain about one kilometer to the north, right in front of you.
When booking the room, a Starbucks coffee coupon was given. Just on the left side of the lobby on the first floor is their banquet center. There is a large tea break area on the first floor, which seems to be in cooperation with Starbucks. I chatted with friends in the tea break area and drank a cup of latte. The environment and coffee taste are great and very comfortable.
Later, I asked their staff. The hotel only opened in October last year. The overall design concept and decoration level of the hotel are very online. All facilities are very new. I almost forgot to say that their service is also very good. In our two rooms, they took the initiative to send us fruits, bananas, cherry tomatoes, and longans. It was great. Five-star praise. Next time I come here on a business trip, I will definitely stay here again.
